# Weapons

Weapons are used to fight Mobs in a player-versus-enemy (PvE) setting.
The type of weapon affects what Enchantments and Reforges can be used on it.

## Weapon Types

### Swords
Swords are melee or magical weapons that deals damage to an enemy. It involves hitting the enemy using a LEFT CLICK , or activating some ability through a RIGHT CLICK .

### Bows
Bows are ranged weapons that require ammunition in the inventory or Quiver .

### Wands
Wands are magical weapons that uses magic abilities for purposes such as healing the player and attacking enemies, the abilities are activated using RIGHT CLICK .

## Trivia
- Some weapons in SkyBlock are references to other games, either on the Hypixel Network (most being from Mega Walls ) or from external games (such as League of Legends ).

# Armor

Armor is a category of equippable items that increase a player's stats when put into the appropriate Armor slot. Armor comes in 4 categories: Helmets , Chestplates , Leggings and Boots . Most Armor pieces come in sets, with one of each type of Armor , however there are also some pieces that are unique and do not belong to any set.

## Mechanics
Most Armor sets grant stats, and the majority of armor sets have a Full Set Bonus , which applies when all pieces in a set are worn. Other pieces also have a Tiered Set Bonus, where the armor set improves the more pieces are worn, but doesn't necessarily require the whole set for the Tiered Set Bonus to work.
The Wardrobe can be used to store and freely swap between sets of Armor.

## Armor Upgrades
These upgrades can be applied to any armor piece, increasing its stats and boosts.
  Example
  Image
  Upgrade
  Description
  Reforges
  Reforges range in effects, and give stats, and sometimes an extra ability. The power of the reforge depending on the Rarity of the item. Reforges cost more coins to apply at higher rarities.
  Enchantments
  Enchantments grant a variety of effects and stat boosts, and some give extra abilities. They can be applied to Armor in an Anvil, and cost Experience to combine.
  Ultimate Enchantments
  Ultimate Enchantments are better than ordinary enchantments, and give a unique, and usually powerful, bonus. However, only one Ultimate Enchantment can be applied per piece.
  Hot Potato Book
  Hot Potato Books grant +4 ❤ Health and +2 ❈ Defense each. They can be applied up to 10 times per piece.
  Fuming Potato Book
  Fuming Potato Books function the same way as Hot Potato Books, as they grant +4 ❤ Health and +2 ❈ Defense each. Can be applied up to 5 times on a piece of armor, on top of the bonus from Hot Potato Books.
  The Art of Peace
  The Art of Peace can be applied once to an armor piece to grant +40 ❤ Health .
  Recombobulator 3000
  Recombobulator 3000 s upgrade the rarity of an armor piece by 1 , thus amplifying its reforge power. They can only be used once per piece.
  Gemstone
  Gemstones add stats to items. They can only be applied to pieces with a corresponding Gemstone Slot . Their power ranges depending on the tier of Gemstone.
  Essence
  Essence can be used to dungeonize and star armor. This grants an extra stat boost when inside a Dungeon
  Master Star
  Master Stars can be used to further dungeonize an armor piece. This goes up to an additional 5 stars, and gives a larger stat boost when inside Master Mode Dungeons.
  Attributes
  Attributes are special items that can be applied to armor pieces. They give small stat bonuses, and some have special abilities. They go from level 1 to 10 .
  Stars
  Certain armor pieces can be starred , which means they can be upgraded into a higher tier version of the same item, but has much better stats.
  Runes
  Runes are purely cosmetic items that can be applied to certain armor pieces to give them particle  effects.

## Armor
- Armor Sets
- Dungeon Sets
- Helmets
- Chestplates
- Leggings
- Boots

### Vanilla Armor
This is the original Minecraft armor. Defense point values correspond to the number of armor points given in vanilla gameplay. These armor sets are recommended to be never used, s of there being much better alternatives.

## Trivia
- The Full Set Bonus of certain armor sets  can be turned off by middle clicking an armor piece in your inventory while wearing it. This will last until you next swap or unequip at least a single armor piece.

# Reforge

# Accessories

Accessories are a category of items that grant buffs while held in a player's inventory or Accessory Bag .

## Mechanics

### Accessory Lines
Accessories come in groups known as Accessory Lines, with some accessories only being the only one in their line, such as Potato Talisman and some who have tiers such as Intimidation Talisman all the way to Intimidation Relic , each tier often comes with a higher rarity than its predecessor and often better stats and perks, only the best accessory from each accessory line will have its buffs and Magical Power count.
A lot of Accessories share a naming path to indicate where it stands in the Accessory Line, most often shown as: Talisman → Ring → Artifact → Relic.
However, there are exceptions to the rule, such as accessories that start as Ring or Artifact instead of Talisman, some that end at Ring or Artifact, some that are the only one in their Accessory Line with no higher or lower tiers, and some that don't use this naming path at all.
There is also an Accessory Line in The Rift that goes beyond Relic , the Crux Talisman , which upgrades past the Crux Relic to the Crux Heirloom , the Crux Chronomicon , and finally the Celestial Starstone .
Accessories in the player's Ender Chest , Backpack , Personal Vault , or Private Island chests will not provide any of their buffs or Magical Power.

### Stats and Perks
Accessories grant various perks, each unique to the accessory, some grant stats, some have abilities and some don't have any at all and only exist to benefit from other ways such as Magical Power.

### Magical Power
When an Accessory is placed in the Accessory Bag it adds Magical Power to the player depending on the rarity of the Accessory which makes Recombing the Accessory grant more Magical Power. Magical Power influences the stats given from Power Stones and points in Stats Tuning .
Only one accessory per accessory line will grant Magical Power, so if the player has two of the same accessory or an upgraded variant only the highest tier accessory will count.
Some Accessories have different rules to how they grant Magical Power:
- Hegemony Artifact grants double the Magical Power its worth
- Rift Prism grants 11 Magical Power when given to Erihann
- Abicases grant +1 Magical Power per 2 contacts in the player's Abiphone

### Enrichments
Enrichments are items that give small bonuses to LEGENDARY and higher accessories. They can be bought from Elizabeth for 5,000 Bits each or from the Auction House. Players can change the enrichments on all of their enriched accessories with an Accessory Enrichment Swapper .

### Priority
If more than one accessory from the same Accessory Line are held, only the effects and Magical Power of the highest tier count. For example, if a player has the Feather Talisman , Feather Ring , and Feather Artifact simultaneously, only the Feather Artifact 's effects and Magical Power count.
The only exceptions are the abilities of Personal Compactors and Personal Deletors , which can all work simultaneously with their separate configurations. However, only one of each will grant Magical Power.

### Upgrading
  Slot
  Upgrade
  Effect
  Notes
  Recombobulator 3000
  Can be used in a Reforge Anvil or at the Dungeon Blacksmith to permanently increase the rarity of an Accessory by +1 .
  An item's rarity can only be upgraded once!
  Enrichment
  Can be combined in an Anvil with a LEGENDARY or higher Accessory to enrich it with the power of a stat.
  Only ONE enrichment can be applied to a given accessory.
  Gemstone
  Can be combined in the Gemstone Grinder with an Accessory with its respective Gemstone Slot to grant a small stat boost.
  Only certain accessories accept gemstones!

## Accessories
- Collection Crafts
- Other Crafts

- Miscellaneous

## Trivia
- When the game was first released to the Prototype Lobby, there were only a few talismans. Later, more types of accessories, like Rings, were added. To avoid confusion, this category of items was retroactively renamed to accessories ; however, some players still use the misnomer talisman instead of accessory .
- There used to be many bugs in the game that allowed the use of different tiers of the same family at a time. These have now been fixed.
- There are, as of SkyBlock 0.24 , 136 Accessories in the game (excluding their own upgrades) and the maximum Magical Power is 1963 Magical Power and another 240 Magical Power from Dungeon Accessories, adding up to 2203 Magical Power in Dungeons . On top of that, 76 Accessories can be Enriched .
- If an accessory has player head texture, it can be worn on player's head, which will make it give stats, but not Magical Power. Wearing an accessory on one's head and having it in Accessory Bag, will only grant stats once. Hatcessories on the other hand can grant the stats twice if worn on head and in Accessory Bag.

# Hyperion

The Hyperion is a LEGENDARY Sword . It is one of four refined Necron's Blade variants, alongside the Valkyrie , Astraea and Scylla . The Hyperion gives a bonus 300 ✎ Intelligence , though it loses 10 ❁ Damage in total.
The Hyperion also grants +1 ❁ Damage and +2 ✎ Intelligence per Catacombs level of the player. As with any Necron's Blade , it deals +50% damage to ☠ Wither mobs.

## Obtaining

### Crafting
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting recipe
  8x L.A.S.R.'s Eye 1x Necron's Blade (Unrefined)
- 8x L.A.S.R.'s Eye
- 1x Necron's Blade (Unrefined)

## Usage

### Crafting
It can be crafted into another Necron's Blade variant using the corresponding recipe, keeping all enchantments and upgrades, though the other items used in the recipe are consumed.
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting recipe
  1x Hyperion and one of the following: 8x Jolly Pink Rock 8x Diamante's Handle 8x Bigfoot's Bola
- 1x Hyperion
- 8x Jolly Pink Rock
- 8x Diamante's Handle
- 8x Bigfoot's Bola
It can have Necron's Blade Scrolls applied to it, granting their effects on right click.

## Essence Crafting
  Essence Required Wither Essence
  Action
  Cost
  Cumul.
  ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪
  150
  150
  ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪

  1,850 10,000 coins
  ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪
  1,500 25,000 coins
  3,350 35,000 coins

## Trivia
- The name "Hyperion" is a reference to the Greek Titan Hyperion , the Titan of light, in Greek mythology.
- The Heroic and Suspicious reforges pair well with the Hyperion . The Fabled reforge is also useful for Left-Click Mage .
- The Fabled reforge is also useful for Left-Click Mage .
- Donating the Hyperion to the Museum gives credit for all Necron's Blade variants.

# Necron's Blade

Necron's Blade is a LEGENDARY Dungeon Sword .

## Stats
See Template:WeaponInfo for more info on how to use the data Module.
  ! Weapon V E D
  Necron's Blade

## Obtaining
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting recipe
  The Catacombs - Floor VII Completion
  24x Wither Catalyst 1x Necron's Handle
- 24x Wither Catalyst
- 1x Necron's Handle
  12 12

## Usage
Necron's Blade can be upgraded to one of 4 refined versions: Hyperion , Astraea , Scylla and Valkyrie . Each refined version is crafted using their respective Precursor Relics dropped from Giants that spawn in The Catacombs - Floor VII Blood Room.
Each of the refined versions specialize in different stats:
- Hyperion grants +350 ✎ Intelligence
- Astraea grants +250 ❈ Defense and +20 ❂ True Defense
- Scylla grants +12% ☣ Crit Chance and +35% ☠ Crit Damage
- Valkyrie grants +60 ⫽ Ferocity
Furthermore, the refined swords keep the passive +50% ❁ Damage to ☠ Wither mobs, alongside a new ability that grants the sword +1 ❁ Damage and +1-2 of the sword's respective stat per Catacombs level.
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting recipe
  The Catacombs - Floor VII Completion
  8x Bigfoot's Bola (for Scylla ) Diamante's Handle (for Valkyrie ) 8x L.A.S.R.'s Eye (for Hyperion 8x Jolly Pink Rock (for Astraea )
Variants of Necron's Blade can also convert between each other using the appropriate Precursor Relic . For example, a Hyperion can be converted to a Valkyrie by using 8x Diamante's Handle .

## Essence Crafting
  Essence Required wither Essence
  Action
  Cost
  Cumul.
  ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪

  ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪ ✪
  1,500 25,000 coins
  3,350 35,000 coins
All 4 variants have the same essence crafting costs.

## Necron's Blade Scrolls
Necron's Blade Scrolls are items that can be applied onto a Necron's Blade to give it abilities on right click. There are 3 scrolls: Implosion , Wither Shield , and Shadow Warp . Multiple scrolls can be applied to the same blade. Applying all 3 to the same blade combines the scrolls into a different ability, Wither Impact .

## Trivia
- The 4 refined swords all have Norse or Greek names from mythology.
- Donating any of the 4 refined swords to the Museum gives credit for Necron's Blade (Unrefined) , but donating a Necron's Blade (Unrefined) does not give credit for any of the Refined swords. The best way to get credit for all 5 items with the minimum amount of donations is to donate a Hyperion .
- The best way to get credit for all 5 items with the minimum amount of donations is to donate a Hyperion .

# Livid Dagger

The Livid Dagger is a LEGENDARY Dungeon Sword .

## Stats
  Sword V E D
  Livid Dagger ❁ Damage : +210 ☣ Crit Chance : +100 ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed : +50 ☠ Crit Damage : +50 ❁ Strength : +60
- ❁ Damage : +210
- ☣ Crit Chance : +100
- ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed : +50
- ☠ Crit Damage : +50
- ❁ Strength : +60
  Effects
  Your Critical Hits deal 100% more damage if you are behind your target. Ability: Throw RIGHT CLICK Throw your dagger at your enemies! Mana Cost: 150 Cooldown: 5s

## Obtaining

### Livid Collection
A Livid Dagger can be claimed once as a reward from Livid III , which is obtained after killing Livid 150 times.

### Dungeon Reward Chests
The Livid Dagger has a small chance to drop in Obsidian or Bedrock Dungeon Post-Boss Chests on the The Catacombs - Floor V . It costs 7,000,000 coins to purchase.
  Reward Chest
  Drop Chance
  Cost
  Default
  S+
  Obsidian
  0.31%
  7,000,000 coins
  Bedrock
  1.16%
  7,000,000 coins
  Obsidian ( Master )
  0.3%
  7,000,000 coins
  Bedrock ( Master )
  1.38%
  2.21%
  7,000,000 coins

## Usage
The Livid Dagger , being a sword, can be used as a melee weapon. It has the unique property of increasing the damage of the wielder's critical hits by +100% if they are behind their target.
Its Throw ability allows the wielder to throw their sword forward, dealing damage to enemies in its path.

  Essence Required Wither Essence

## Tips
- Applying the Fast reforge to a Livid Dagger allows it to reach +100% ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed .

## History
  SkyBlock Prototype
  Sep 17, 2020
  0.9.1
  Added Livid Dagger .
  Sep 24, 2020
  Passive +50% damage and +150% damage from behind changed to only +100% damage from behind.
  Added +50 ☠ Crit Damage .
  Item Ability can now deal critical damage.
  Fixed all hits on Ender Dragons being counted as backstabs.
  Decreased drop rate from Obsidian Chests.
  Cost increased by 2,000,000 coins (from 5,000,000 coins to 7,000,000 coins ).
  Sep 28, 2022
  0.15
  Nerfed ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed from 100% to 50%.

# Terminator

The Terminator is a LEGENDARY Bow that can be obtained via Crafting . Its recipe can be unlocked upon reaching Enderman Slayer VII . It fires arrows rapidly and has a unique ability.

## Stats
See Template:WeaponInfo for more info on how to use the data Module.
  ! Weapon V E D
  Terminator

## Obtaining

### Crafting
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting recipe
  Enderman Slayer VII
  1x Judgement Core 3x Null Blade 4x Braided Griffin Feather 8x Tessellated Ender Pearl 128x Tarantula Silk
- 1x Judgement Core
- 3x Null Blade
- 4x Braided Griffin Feather
- 8x Tessellated Ender Pearl
- 128x Tarantula Silk
  4 64 4 4 64

## Usage
The Terminator is a ranged weapon, capable of hitting Enderman . Players must reach Enderman Slayer VII to be able to use this weapon.
It is a shortbow, meaning it fires arrows instantly without the need to charge. Holding down right-click allows it to continuously fire. The maximum rate of fire is determined by the player's ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed .
It fires 3 arrows per shot, 1 straight and 2 spread at 5°, a tighter spread than Runaan's Bow and the inner arrows of the Hurricane Bow and Venom's Touch . The side arrows do the same damage as the middle arrow. The Archer class Doubleshot passive only affects the middle arrow and will not fire additional side arrows.
After landing 3 hits on enemies, The Salvation ability can be cast with left click. The beam is similar to that of the Precursor Eye 's, having a range of 32 blocks. The beam can hit up to 5 enemies, These enemies are dealt arrow damage. This beam is guaranteed to do critical damage regardless of ☣ Crit Chance . This ability costs 1 ⸎ Soulflow . When the bow is held and the Salvation ability is off cooldown, a colored text indicator appears on the action bar indicating when the ability is ready to be used. Its status is indicated as T1 , T2 and T3! . The beam is ready to fire when T3! shows. The ability has a 0.25 second cooldown.
Unlike other bows, when held, it divides its user's ☣ Crit Chance by 4, meaning you only get 25% of ☣ Crit Chance from all sources.

## Fire Rate
When left-clicking, the fire rate starts at 2.22 shots per second (9 ticks per shot) with 0 ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed and increases to 5 shots per second (4 ticks per shot) with 100 ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed . The increase in fire rate with ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed is incremental, not continuous. The maximum possible fire rate that can be achieved by optimal left-clicking depending on the player's ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed :
  Ticks per shot
  ⚔ Bonus Attack Speed
  Shots per second
  Lowest
  Highest
  9 (0.45s)
  < -8
  11
  2.22
  7 (0.35s)

## Essence Crafting
This weapon can be upgraded with Dragon Essence. Once converted, it requires Catacombs 27 to use while in Catacombs .

## Trivia
- Contrary to the weapon's description, the ability only deals the same damage as an arrow, instead of x2 damage
- The item's crafting recipe was changed after it was added, adding the Judgement Core to its recipe.
- Prior to Update 0.19, the Terminator required the highest amount of raw materials to craft in the game, at 14,450,332 raw materials. The earliest version of the crafting recipe required 20,866,742 raw materials. As of 0.19, the Tier XI Inferno Minion and SOS Flare requires more amount of raw materials, at 303,596,064 and 148,659,281 raw materials respectively
- The earliest version of the crafting recipe required 20,866,742 raw materials.
- As of 0.19, the Tier XI Inferno Minion and SOS Flare requires more amount of raw materials, at 303,596,064 and 148,659,281 raw materials respectively
- When left-clicking on a mob in melee range, arrows will not be fired. Right-clicking will fire arrows as intended.
- The middle arrow of the bow suffers from bow inaccuracy like all other bows. However, the side arrows will always come out perfectly at 5° to the crosshair.
- This, along with the Juju Shortbow , were the first Shortbows to be released.
- The Terminator's Salvation Ability can hit Decoys and Thorn , but not damage them.
- Prior to the 0.16.1 update, the recipe included 3 stacked Null Blades, which was impossible to obtain. This made the bow only craftable through Quick Craft and thus only be able to be crafted by players with a Hypixel Rank.

## History
  Sep 2, 2022
  AHN 0.15
  Now displays shot cooldown in lore.
  SkyBlock Prototype
  May 31, 2021
  0.11.5
  Added Terminator .
  June 3, 2021
  Changed recipe from 8 Tesselated Ender Pearls , 6 Null Blades , 4 Braided Griffin Feathers , 128 Tarantula Silk to 8 Tesselated Ender Pearls , 4 Null Blades , 4 Braided Griffin Feathers , 128 Tarantula Silk , 1 Judgement Core .
  -25 ❁ Damage (from 335 to 310).
  Decreased amount of Null Blades in crafting recipe from 4 to 3.
  Aug 17, 2021
  Fixed being able to bypass the Slayer level requirement when the item is dungeonized and used within Dungeons.
  Sep 7, 2021
  Fixed the side arrows not shooting. This bug had been active for about 4 hours prior to the fix.
  Nov 9, 2022
  0.16.1
  Changed the recipe to allow players without a rank to craft it without Quick Craft (same amount of items).
  Sep 12, 2023
  0.19.4
  Changed Salvation to be activated by Left Click (from Right click). Cooldown increased by 0.25 second (From 0)

# Aspect of the Dragons

The Aspect of the Dragons , commonly abbreviated as AOTD , is a LEGENDARY Sword dropped from an Ender Dragon . Its ability deals damage and knocks back enemies.

## Stats
  Sword V E D
  Aspect of the Dragons ❁ Damage : +225 ❁ Strength : +100
- ❁ Damage : +225
- ❁ Strength : +100
  Effects
  Ability: Dragon Rage RIGHT CLICK Deal 12,000 ๑ Ability Damage to all Monsters in front of you. Damaged Monsters Take Huge Knockback. Mana Cost: 100

## Obtaining
The Aspect of the Dragons is obtained by defeating any Ender Dragon in the ⏣ Dragon's Nest (except Superior) located at the bottom of ⏣ The End . 8x Summoning Eyes need to be placed to summon the Ender Dragon and players need to have 450 Dragon Weight to have a chance of getting the sword. The sword has a 3% drop chance per eye placed.

## Usage
At least Combat XVIII (18) , and if converted into a dungeon item, Catacombs XII (12) is required to use this item.
When its ability is used, it produces a fiery cone 7.5 blocks long and 60° wide. All enemies within the cone take 12,000 ๑ Ability Damage and take extremely heavy knockback. This knockback is effectively infinite, meaning mobs are knocked until they are stopped by a wall. The ability costs 100 ✎ Mana to use and has no cooldown.
Slayer bosses, Mythological Creatures and Sea Creatures are unaffected by the ability.

## Trivia
- This weapon's stats can be further boosted by the Ender Dragon Pet , with a maximum of an additional 50 ❁ Damage and 30 ❁ Strength .
- The Dragonfuse Glove gives Aspect of the Dragons 35 ❁ Damage , 50 ❁ Strength , and significantly reduces the Dragon Rage repelling.
- The name may be a reference to the buff from the game League of Legends called "Aspect of the Dragon".
- For a long time, this sword was considered the second-best sword after the 50 million Midas Sword . However, many swords from Dungeons such as the Livid Dagger , Giant's Sword , Hyperion , and Valkyrie now outclass this weapon.
- Previously, the Dragon Rage ability was effective against Dragons . What that means is if the ability was used on a Dragon, it would be blasted away completely, leaving only the boss bar up top. No other Dragons could be spawned during this time, and it would stay that way until the server was reset. Gregory would also stay there until the server was reset since there was still a dragon fight in progress. However, this was patched in a later update.
- In Patch 0.9.10 , Sea Creatures could no longer be affected by Dragon Rage . This made fishing a lot less painful as Great White Shark s, Sea Emperor s, and Yeti s could no longer be knocked into their despawn range or into the void by griefers.
- The Lost Adventurer mini-boss in The Catacombs attacks with an Aspect of the Dragons and occasionally uses the Dragon Rage ability, although in chat it is displayed as "Dragon's Breath".
- Aspect of the Dragons is a reference to Dragon Sword in another Hypixel minigame, UHC Champions.
- The Dragon Rage might be based on the Pokémon move of the same name .

# Wither Armor

The Wither Armor is a LEGENDARY Dungeon Armor set that can be obtained from post-boss chests in The Catacombs - Floor VII .

  Effects
  Reduces the damage you take from withers by 10% . Full Set Bonus: Witherborn Spawns a wither minion every 30 seconds up to a maximum of 1 wither. Your withers will travel to and explode on nearby enemies.

## Obtaining

### Dungeon Reward Chests
Wither Armor can be obtained from Dungeon Reward Chest within The Catacombs - Floor VII . When picked up, it has a chance to be upgraded with 1-5 stars, Growth VI , Protection VI , and/or Recombobulated .

### Necron Collection
The Wither Helmet, Chestplate and Leggings can be obtained as rewards through the Necron Collection.
- Wither Helmet : Necron III , after killing Necron 150 times
- Wither Chestplate : Necron VI , after killing Necron 750 times
- Wither Leggings' : Necron V , after killing Necron 500 times

## Usage

### Crafting
Wither Armor can be upgraded into Storm's , Goldor's , Maxor's , or Necron's Armor , by surrounding any piece with any 8 of the respective Precursor Relics .
- Storm's Armor is created with L.A.S.R.'s Eye and increases ✎ Intelligence .
- Goldor's Armor is created with Jolly Pink Rock and increases ❤ Health and ❈ Defense .
- Maxor's Armor is created with Bigfoot's Bola and increases ✦ Speed and ☠ Crit Damage .
- Necron's Armor is created with Diamante's Handle and increases ❁ Strength and ☠ Crit Damage .
Upgrading the armor will keep all existing upgrades such as stars, reforges, potato books and enchantments. Variants of Wither Armor can also be converted between each other using the appropriate Precursor Relic.
  Maxor's Armor
  Goldor's Armor
  Storm's Armor
  Necron's Armor

## Gallery

## Trivia
- When the armor was first released, crafting Wither Armor into its upgraded form would keep the color code of #000000 , creating incredibly rare, "exotic" colored armor. On March 1st, 2022, an update was released, containing a bug that caused the same thing to happen, making colored armor worth much less. This was patched within a few hours, but many new black variants were created in that time. Since the release of Pure Black Dye , these armor sets aren't exclusive anymore, but they still won't be easy to get as each dye costs 250,000 Bits .
- On March 1st, 2022, an update was released, containing a bug that caused the same thing to happen, making colored armor worth much less. This was patched within a few hours, but many new black variants were created in that time. Since the release of Pure Black Dye , these armor sets aren't exclusive anymore, but they still won't be easy to get as each dye costs 250,000 Bits .
- This was patched within a few hours, but many new black variants were created in that time. Since the release of Pure Black Dye , these armor sets aren't exclusive anymore, but they still won't be easy to get as each dye costs 250,000 Bits .
- Since the release of Pure Black Dye , these armor sets aren't exclusive anymore, but they still won't be easy to get as each dye costs 250,000 Bits .
- DIVINE (previously SUPREME ) Wither Armor and its variants were possible to obtain if the armor was glitched and was recombobulated twice from opening Dungeon Reward Chest .
- Sometimes while a player is a ghost in dungeons, the full set ability will still spawn and explode on enemies.
- Donating any of the 4 Wither Armor variants to the Museum gives credit for Wither Armor , but donating Wither Armor does not give credit for any of the variants. The best way to get credit for all 5 items with the minimum amount of donations is to donate Necron's Armor .
- The best way to get credit for all 5 items with the minimum amount of donations is to donate Necron's Armor .

# Necron's Armor

Necron's Armor is a LEGENDARY Armor set and an upgraded variant of Wither Armor named after Necron . It is obtained from The Catacombs - Floor VII and provides great ❤ Effective Health as well as ❁ Strength and ☠ Crit Damage .

## Stats
  Armor Set V E D
  Helmet
  Chestplate
  Necron's Helmet ❁ Strength : +40 ☠ Crit Damage : +30 ❈ Defense : +100 ❤ Health : +180 ✎ Intelligence : +30

- ☠ Crit Damage : +120

  Effects
  Reduces the damage you take from withers by 10% . Full Set Bonus: Witherborn Spawns a wither minion every 30 seconds up to a maximum of 1 wither. Your withers will travel to and explode on nearby enemies.

## Gallery

## Trivia
- The wither spawned from the Witherborn full set bonus can be teleported to by using a Shadow Fury or a Silent Death .
- Many players choose to replace the Necron's Chestplate with cheaper alternatives such as the Zombie Knight Chestplate and or a Shadow Assassin Chestplate , sometimes using a Necromancer Lord Chestplate .
- Many players choose to replace the Necron's Helmet with a Golden or Diamond Necron Head , Tarantula Helmet or Primordial Helmet , or a Warden Helmet .
- The Necron Dye can be obtained from Master Mode Floor VII , which can change the color of Leather Armor to #E7413C , which is the color of Necron's Chestplate .
- Donating Necron's Armor to the Museum grants credit for all other Wither Armor variants.
